This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. \n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n188:     \"\"\"\n189:     + rf\"\"\"\n190:     Args:\n191: This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n245: \n246:     \"\"\"\n247: )\n248: \n249: \n250: def sgd(\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n261:     *,\n262:     weight_decay: float,\n263:     momentum: float,\n264:     lr: float,\n265:     dampening: float,\n266:     nesterov: bool,\n267:     maximize: bool,\n268: ):\n269:     r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n270: \n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n272:     \"\"\"\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. Create a simple model for testing\n        self.model = nn.Linear(10, 5)\n        self.input = torch.randn(8, 10)\n        self.target = torch.randn(8, 5)\n        self.criterion = nn.MSELoss()\n\n    def test_gradient_noise_injector_with_sgd(self):\n        \"\"\"Test GradientNoiseInjector wraps SGD optimizer.\"\"\"\n        optimizer = SGD(self.model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        noisy_optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        # Test variance computation at different steps\n        variances = []\n        for t in range(5):\n            noisy_optimizer.step_count = t\n            sigma = noisy_optimizer._compute_sigma()\n            variance = sigma ** 2\n            variances.append(variance)\n\n            # Verify formula: sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n            expected_variance = eta / ((1 + t) ** gamma)\n            self.assertAlmostEqual(variance, expected_variance, places=5)\n\n        # Verify that variance decreases monotonically\n        for i in range(len(variances) - 1):\n            self.assertGreater(variances[i], variances[i + 1])\n\n    def test_noise_injection_occurs(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that noise is actually injected into gradients.\"\"\"\n        # Create a deterministic model\n        torch.manual_seed(42)\n        model = nn.Linear(10, 5)\n        optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        noisy_optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(optimizer, eta=0.1, gamma=0.0)\n\n        # Get initial gradient values\n        input_data = torch.randn(8, 10)\n        target = torch.randn(8, 5)\n        criterion = nn.MSELoss()\n\n        # Run two optimization steps with the same input/target\n        # and collect the gradient magnitudes before noise injection\n        gradients_without_injection = []\n        gradients_with_injection = []\n\n        # First step: record gradients after noise injection\n        loss = criterion(model(input_data), target)\n        loss.backward()\n\n        # Save gradients before step (which injects noise)\n        grads_before = [p.grad.clone() if p.grad is not None else None\n                        for p in model.parameters()]\n\n        noisy_optimizer.step()\n\n        # Reset for second iteration\n        noisy_optimizer.zero_grad()\n        model.load_state_dict(model.state_dict())  # Reset model state\n\n        loss = criterion(model(input_data), target)\n        loss.backward()\n\n        grads_second = [p.grad.clone() if p.grad is not None else None\n                        for p in model.parameters()]\n\n        # The gradients should be the same before noise injection\n        # but the optimizer step would be different if noise was injected\n        for g1, g2 in zip(grads_before, grads_second):\n            if g1 is not None and g2 is not None:\n                # Gradients should be numerically equal (same input/target)\n                self.assertTrue(torch.allclose(g1, g2, rtol=1e-4))\n\n    def test_zero_grad(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that zero_grad delegates to base optimizer.\"\"\"\n        optimizer = SGD(self.model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        noisy_optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(optimizer)\n\n        # Compute gradients\n        loss = self.criterion(self.model(self.input), self.target)\n        loss.backward()\n\n        # Check that gradients are not None\n        for p in self.model.parameters():\n            self.assertIsNotNone(p.grad)\n\n        # {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_016NjFmVwoCY1JKUFMpXJEvu","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01TCfYWfGrHuBUgXgTwDvZKW","name":"Bash","input":{"command":"cat > /tmp/code_review.md << 'EOF'\n# GradientNoiseInjector Implementation - Code Review\n\n## Summary\nSuccessfully implemented `GradientNoiseInjector` - an optimizer wrapper that adds calibrated Gaussian noise to gradients before the optimizer step, implementing the \"Adding Gradient Noise Improves Learning for Very Deep Networks\" technique.\n\n## Key Implementation Features\n\n### 1. Noise Schedule Formula ✓\n```python\ndef _compute_sigma(self) -> float:\n    t = self.step_count\n    variance = self.eta / ((1 + t) ** self.gamma)\n    return float(variance**0.5)\n```\n- Correctly implements: σ² = η / (1 + t)^γ\n- Variance decays with each step (monotonic decrease)\n- Returns standard deviation (square root of variance)\n\n### 2. Noise Injection ✓\n```python\ndef _inject_noise(self) -> None:\n    sigma = self._compute_sigma()\n    for group in self.optimizer.param_groups:\n        for p in group[\"params\"]:\n            if p.grad is not None:\n                noise = torch.randn_like(p.grad) * sigma\n                p.grad.add_(noise)\n```\n- Uses `torch.randn_like()` for Gaussian noise generation\n- Iterates through all parameter groups\n- Adds noise in-place to existing gradients\n- Checks for None gradients (safety check)\n\n### 3. Step Coordination ✓\n```python\ndef step(self, closure: Optional[Callable] = None) -> Optional[Tensor]:\n    self._inject_noise()           # 1. Inject noise\n    self.step_count += 1            # 2. Increment counter\n    return self.optimizer.step(closure)  # 3. Delegate to base optimizer\n```\n- Noise injection happens BEFORE base optimizer step\n- Step count incremented at correct time\n- Delegates closure handling to base optimizer\n\n### 4. Wrapper Pattern ✓\n```python\ndef __getattr__(self, name):\n    return getattr(self.optimizer, name)\n```\n- Allows transparent access to base optimizer attributes\n- Supports both `optimizer.param_groups` (used in noise injection)\n- Enables dynamic delegation of unknown methods\n\n### 5. State Management ✓\n```python\ndef state_dict(self):\n    return {\n        \"state_dict\": self.optimizer.state_dict(),\n        \"step_count\": self.step_count,\n    }\n\ndef load_state_dict(self, state_dict):\n    self.optimizer.load_state_dict(state_dict[\"state_dict\"])\n    self.step_count = state_dict.get(\"step_count\", 0)\n```\n- Saves/restores both optimizer and wrapper state\n-
